3. Although it is a super high-rise building, the response and operation speed of the six elevators are very fast;
4. The room is neat and clean, cleaned in a timely manner, and replenished with sufficient supplies;
5. Open washroom, the toilet and bathroom are separated without disturbing each other. The bathroom is especially worthy of praise. The hot water comes quickly, the shower head flows smoothly, the faucet does not shake, and the water flow basically does not overflow;
Small areas for improvement:
1. The toilet section lacks hooks, and there is nowhere to hang towels and changes of clothes;
2. The toilet flushing sound is a bit loud;
3. The air conditioner in the room has no quiet air, and the wind at the lowest setting is blowing toward the people on the bed, making it too hot without the air conditioner and too noisy and too cold with the air conditioner on;
4. The pants and mattress are thick in this weather, causing the covered part of the body to be too hot and the exposed part to be too cold.
Overall, the flaws are not hidden, and the overall feeling is very good. I will consider staying here again when I come to Wenzhou again. like! come on!

When I went to the front desk, I showed my ID card. The front desk clerk first questioned whether I had booked the wrong hotel or the wrong date. After I opened the order in the Ctrip app and showed it to him, he fiddled with it on the computer again and said he found it. According to Ctrip's requirements, he upgraded to an executive king bed room type. I thought I would be able to check in right away, but the staff called me to ask: The guest booked the wrong date... I immediately realized that my family and I were people with normal senses, and immediately changed my story and said that the hotel staff had booked the room upgrade date earlier (I booked it earlier) The date was 10-11, but they changed it to 8-9). The order cannot be withdrawn. Do I need to place a new order? After getting the consent, I checked in and was told to upgrade to an executive king bed... and immediately changed to a superior king bed room. My family and I didn't pay attention at the time and took the room card and went to the room. When I got to the room, I found that it didn't look like it had been upgraded, and the sanitation didn't look like it had been done. There were still unknown liquid stains on the toilet seat. So I called the front desk staff who just checked me in. Reply: First of all, the upgraded room is the superior king bed room. It is slightly different from the one I originally booked in terms of area, but everything else is the same. I pointed out that my family and I all heard that it was upgraded to an executive room. So the staff immediately explained that it was because the executive room was being renovated and they were afraid of disturbing our rest, so they changed to a superior room.
I didn‚Äôt want to argue, so I went to eat with my family first. While eating, I received a call from the hotel check-in staff, telling me that I could change rooms. An executive room had been arranged and I was asked to change my room card at that time. After dinner, I went back to the hotel and went to the front desk to change my room card. It can be said that the attitude of the staff was quite polite. At least I said "sorry" and "sorry" many times. After changing the room card, take the elevator to the new room. The room I was given before was 3109 (Superior King Room), but this time I was given an Executive King Room 3220. After opening the door, I found that there was no difference in layout or area from the previous room. Except for the fact that there were no beds and other furniture to deliberately confuse the size like a model room, there would be absolutely no difference. The only two differences are that this time there is an air purifier and the fruit plate that should be in the room (room 3109 did not have it before). Toilet pad hygiene has improved slightly. Because it's too late, I don't want to argue with them anymore. Then it was time to wash up and rest. In the middle, I said that the water in the shower room was really weak (please allow me to say this, it is just a subjective comment). I was watching "Qing Qing Daily" at the time. I thought I was tired of watching it on my iPad. I found that the TV in the room could cast the screen, so I followed the instructions and cast the screen. The effect was pretty good. It didn't last for 5 minutes, but suddenly the content I was casting was exited, and an inexplicable video was cast on the TV in my room. It was very indecent. I immediately tried to cast the program on my iPad, but was quickly interrupted by that picture again, and then inserted N times by the World Cup quarter-finals... The next day, I was first "awakened" by the light through the curtains. ", and then I was disturbed by the passage light turning on inexplicably at 8 o'clock (I didn't make a morning call), and I couldn't sleep anymore...
After breakfast, I went to the front desk to check out. The front desk said: Just give me the room card. Then he and his family wanted to drive away. Halfway through the walk, I was forced to be taken back to the front desk by what seemed to be the foreman, saying "Wait a minute" and "You don't have enough room charges." Then I watched him operate the computer and said, "Sorry, I misread it. It's okay." He signaled to us that we were not here. The problem can be gone.
The above is my experience of checking in at 18:00 on December 10th and checking out at 9:40 on December 11th at Wenzhou Kaiyuan Mingdu Hotel.
